
add_namespace = release_nation_events

country_event = {
	id = release_nation_events.150
	title = release_nation_events.150.t	# Set Ideology Event
	desc = release_nation_events.150.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty3
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.150.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		set_variable = { puppet_fascism_popularity = party_popularity@fascism }
		set_variable = { puppet_democratic_popularity = party_popularity@democratic }
		set_variable = { puppet_communism_popularity = party_popularity@communism }
		set_variable = { puppet_monarchism_popularity = party_popularity@monarchism }
		set_variable = { puppet_neutrality_popularity = 1 }
		subtract_from_variable = { puppet_neutrality_popularity = puppet_fascism_popularity } 
		subtract_from_variable = { puppet_neutrality_popularity = puppet_democratic_popularity } 
		subtract_from_variable = { puppet_neutrality_popularity = puppet_communism_popularity } 
		subtract_from_variable = { puppet_neutrality_popularity = puppet_monarchism_popularity }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
			set_variable = { puppet_ruling_party = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			set_variable = { puppet_ruling_party = 2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			set_variable = { puppet_ruling_party = 3 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			set_variable = { puppet_ruling_party = 4 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = monarchism
			}
			set_variable = { puppet_ruling_party = 5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					original_tag = ENG
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_free } }
					}
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = ENG_guided_by_britain_colony_1
						days = 720
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = ENG_guided_by_britain_colony_2
						days = 360
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = guided_colony_1
				days = 360
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_free } }
				}
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = guided_colony_2
					days = 720
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = already_puppeted
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_puppet }
				}
				FROM = { set_autonomy = { target = ROOT autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_reichsprotectorate }
				}
				FROM = { set_autonomy = { target = ROOT autonomy_state = autonomy_reichsprotectorate } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_dominion }
				}
				FROM = { set_autonomy = { target = ROOT autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion } }
				ROOT = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = ROOT_released_us } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_imperial_protectorate }
				}
				FROM = { set_autonomy = { target = ROOT autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_protectorate } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_imperial_associate }
				}
				FROM = { set_autonomy = { target = ROOT autonomy_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_associate } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_supervised_state }
				}
				FROM = { set_autonomy = { target = ROOT autonomy_state = autonomy_supervised_state } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_satellite }
				}
				FROM = { set_autonomy = { target = ROOT autonomy_state = autonomy_satellite } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_reichskommissariat }
				}
				FROM = { set_autonomy = { target = ROOT autonomy_state = autonomy_reichskommissariat } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_colony }
				}
				FROM = { set_autonomy = { target = ROOT autonomy_state = autonomy_colony } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_integrated_puppet }
				}
				FROM = { set_autonomy = { target = ROOT autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet } }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_faction_member }
				}
				ROOT = {
					add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = ROOT_released_us }
					if = {
						limit = {
							FROM = { is_in_faction = yes }
						}
						FROM = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
					}
					else = {
						FROM = {
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = ROOT
								relation = guarantee
								active = yes
							}
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = ROOT
								relation = military_access
								active = yes
							}
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = ROOT
								relation = docking_rights
								active = yes
							}
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = ROOT
								relation = non_aggression_pact
								active = yes
							}
						}
						ROOT = {
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = FROM
								relation = guarantee
								active = yes
							}
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = FROM
								relation = military_access
								active = yes
							}
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = FROM
								relation = docking_rights
								active = yes
							}
							diplomatic_relation = {
								country = FROM
								relation = non_aggression_pact
								active = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { has_country_flag = release_as_free }
				}
				ROOT = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = ROOT_released_us } }
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = already_puppeted
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 100
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = puppet_fascism_popularity
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = puppet_democratic_popularity
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = puppet_communism_popularity
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = monarchism
			popularity = puppet_monarchism_popularity
		}
		set_history_file_government = yes
		set_history_file_government = yes
		set_history_file_government = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { puppet_ruling_party = 1 }
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { puppet_ruling_party = 2 }
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { puppet_ruling_party = 3 }
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { puppet_ruling_party = 4 }
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { puppet_ruling_party = 5 }
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = monarchism
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM.FROM = {
					has_government = fascism
					has_country_flag = release_not_local_rulers
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					fascism < 0.5
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 50
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM.FROM = {
					has_government = democratic
					has_country_flag = release_not_local_rulers
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					democratic < 0.5
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 50
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM.FROM = {
					has_government = communism
					has_country_flag = release_not_local_rulers
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					communism < 0.5
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 50
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM.FROM = {
					has_government = neutrality
					has_country_flag = release_not_local_rulers
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					neutrality < 0.5
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 50
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM.FROM = {
					has_government = monarchism
					has_country_flag = release_not_local_rulers
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = monarchism
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					monarchism < 0.5
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = monarchism
					popularity = 50
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM.FROM = {
					has_government = fascism
					has_country_flag = release_local_rulers
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM.FROM = {
					has_government = democratic
					has_country_flag = release_local_rulers
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM.FROM = {
					has_government = neutrality
					has_country_flag = release_local_rulers
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM.FROM = {
					has_government = communism
					has_country_flag = release_local_rulers
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM.FROM = {
					has_government = monarchism
					has_country_flag = release_local_rulers
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = monarchism
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = release_nation_events.60
	title = release_nation_events.60.t	# Freedom for ANG
	desc = release_nation_events.60.d	#
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty3
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.60.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 540 
		}
		AN0 = {
			transfer_state = 540
			custom_effect_tooltip = defensive_garrison_tooltip
			hidden_effect = { load_oob = "_Independence_ANG" }
			country_event = { id = release_nation_events.150 }
		}
		ROOT = {
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { id = am.news.6 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.nevermind
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = release_nation_events.69
	title = release_nation_events.69.t	# Freedom for TZN
	desc = release_nation_events.69.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty3
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	

	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.69.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 546
			controls_state = 933
		}
		TZ0 = {
			transfer_state = 546
			transfer_state = 933
			custom_effect_tooltip = defensive_garrison_tooltip
			hidden_effect = { load_oob = "_Independence_TZN" }
			country_event = { id = release_nation_events.150 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				548 = {
					is_core_of = TZ0
				}
			}
			TZ0 = {
				remove_state_core = 548
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				934 = {
					is_core_of = TZ0
				}
			}
			TZ0 = {
				remove_state_core = 934
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				547 = {
					is_core_of = TZ0
				}
			}
			TZ0 = {
				remove_state_core = 547
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				928 = {
					is_core_of = TZ0
				}
			}
			TZ0 = {
				remove_state_core = 928
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				768 = {
					is_core_of = TZ0
				}
			}
			TZ0 = {
				remove_state_core = 768
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				769 = {
					is_core_of = TZ0
				}
			}
			TZ0 = {
				remove_state_core = 769
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TZ0 = { has_cosmetic_tag = TZN_federation }
			}
			TZ0 = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TZ0 = {
					capital_scope = {
						NOT = { state = 546 }
					}
				}
			}
			TZ0 = { set_capital = 546 }
		}
		ROOT = {
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { id = am.news.15 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.nevermind
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = release_nation_events.70

		ROOT = {

			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.nevermind
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = release_nation_events.73
	title = release_nation_events.73.t	# Freedom for ERI 1
	desc = release_nation_events.73.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty3
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.73.a 
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 550
			controls_state = 915
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_government = communism }
					NOT = { original_tag = ET0 }
					ET0 = {
						owns_state = 271
						controls_state = 271
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ER0 = {
			transfer_state = 550
			transfer_state = 915
			custom_effect_tooltip = defensive_garrison_tooltip

		}
		ROOT = {
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { id = am.news.19 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.73.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_government = communism
					original_tag = ET0
					ET0 = { NOT = { owns_state = 271 } }
					ET0 = { NOT = { controls_state = 271 } }
					ET0 = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 550
			controls_state = 915
			NOT = { original_tag = ET0 }
			ET0 = {
				owns_state = 271
				controls_state = 271
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		ER0 = {
			transfer_state = 550
			transfer_state = 915
			custom_effect_tooltip = defensive_garrison_tooltip
			hidden_effect = { load_oob = "_Independence_ERI" }
			set_country_flag = already_puppeted
		}
		ET0 = {
			set_autonomy = { target = ER0 autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion }
			ER0 = { country_event = { id = release_nation_events.150 } }
		}
		ET0 = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = gave_eritrea }
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = gave_eritrea_little
				}
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = gave_western_eritrea
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { id = am.news.20 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.73.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		trigger = {
			controls_state = 550
			controls_state = 915
			NOT = { original_tag = ET0 }
			ET0 = {
				owns_state = 271
				controls_state = 271
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
		}
		ET0 = {
			transfer_state = 550
			transfer_state = 915
		}
		ET0 = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = gave_eritrea }
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = gave_eritrea_little
				}
				remove_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = gave_western_eritrea
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { id = am.news.21 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.moreoptions

			controls_state = 550

		}
	}

			}

country_event = {
	id = release_nation_events.165
	title = release_nation_events.151.t	# Freedom for OMA
	desc = release_nation_events.151.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty3
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = release_nation_events.151.e
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = OM5 }
			NOT = { tag = OM0 }
			controls_state = 294
			controls_state = 922
			controls_state = 919
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = release_as_free
					has_country_flag = release_as_faction_member
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = hold_referendum_oman1_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = hold_referendum_oman2_tooltip
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					OM0 = {
						transfer_state = 294
						transfer_state = 922
						transfer_state = 919
						custom_effect_tooltip = defensive_garrison_tooltip
						hidden_effect = { load_oob = "_Independence_OMA" }
						country_event = { id = release_nation_events.150 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							controls_state = 921
						}
						OM0 = {
							transfer_state = 921
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							OM0 = { has_cosmetic_tag = OMA_muscat }
						}
						OM0 = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
					}
					ROOT = {
						hidden_effect = {
							news_event = { id = am.news.146 days = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
				40 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								has_country_flag = release_as_free
								has_country_flag = release_as_faction_member
							}
						}
					}
					OM0 = {
						transfer_state = 294
						transfer_state = 922
						custom_effect_tooltip = defensive_garrison_tooltip
						hidden_effect = { load_oob = "_Independence_OMA" }
						country_event = { id = release_nation_events.150 }
						add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = didnt_give_oman }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							controls_state = 921
						}
						OM0 = {
							transfer_state = 921
						}
					}
					OM5 = {
						transfer_state = 919
						custom_effect_tooltip = defensive_garrison_tooltip
						hidden_effect = { load_oob = "_Independence_OMN" }
						set_country_flag = already_puppeted
					}
					OM0 = {
						set_autonomy = { target = OM5 autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion }

					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { OM0 = { has_cosmetic_tag = OMA_muscat } }
						}
						OM0 = { set_cosmetic_tag = OMA_muscat }
					}
					ROOT = {
						hidden_effect = {
							news_event = { id = am.news.170 days = 1 }

					}
				}
				50 = {
					OM0 = {
						transfer_state = 294
